# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.

     4→package format
     5→
     6→import (
     7→	"fmt"
     8→	"sort"
     9→	"strings"
    10→
    11→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    13→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    14→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
    15→)
    16→
    17→// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
    18→// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
    19→// attribute-level detail.
    20→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    21→
    22→// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.
    23→// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.
    24→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    25→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    26→		return ""
    27→	}
    28→
    29→	// Group changes by action type
    30→	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
    31→
    32→	// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects
    33→	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
    34→		// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)
    35→		if rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {
    36→			continue
    37→		}
    38→
    39→		changesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)
    40→	}
    41→
    42→	var output strings.Builder
    43→
    44→	// Define the order of actions to display
    45→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    46→		plans.Create,
    47→		plans.Update,
    48→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    49→		plans.CreateThenDelete,
    50
... (truncated)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
// attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.
// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Group changes by action type
	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)

Perfect! I have successfully implemented the `CompactDiffFormatter` for Terraform. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Implementation Summary

### 1. **`internal/command/format/compact.go`** - Main Formatter Implementation

**Key Features:**
- **CompactDiffFormatter struct** - An empty struct implementing the formatter interface
- **Format method** - Signature: `func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas) string`
  - Returns compact summary output grouped by action type
  - Filters out deposed objects (only shows current objects)
  - Handles all plan actions: Create, Update, Delete, DeleteThenCreate, CreateThenDelete, Read, Forget, CreateThenForget

**Output Format:**
```
Create resources:
  [+] resource_type.name
  [+] another_resource.name

Update resources:
  [~] resource_type.name

Delete resources:
  [-] resource_type.name

Plan: X to add, Y to change, Z to destroy
```

**Helper Functions:**
- `actionLabel()` - Maps action types to human-readable labels
- `actionSymbol()` - Returns symbols for actions (e.g., `+`, `-`, `~`, `-/+`, `+/-`)
- `countChanges()` - Aggregates change counts by action type

### 2. **`internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** - Comprehensive Test Suite

**Test Coverage:**
- Empty plan handling
- Single resource changes (create, update, delete)
- Mixed changes across multiple actions
- Replace operations (DeleteThenCreate, CreateThenDelete)
- Deposed object filtering
- Resource sorting by address
- All action types (Read, Forget, CreateThenForget)
- Nil plan and nil changes handling

**Test Framework:**
- Uses Go's standard `testing` package
- Employs `google.com/go-cmp/cmp` for output comparison
- Helper function `makeAddr()` to parse resource addresses

Process each action type in order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges, ok := changesByAction[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel fmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s\", resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"module.%s.%s.%s\", strings.Join(rc.Addr.Module.Module().Names(), \".\"), resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\toutput.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tcounts := destroy\\n\",\n\t\tcounts[plans.Create]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]+counts[plans.CreateThenForget],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Update],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Delete]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete],\n\t))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, type\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"-/+\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"+/-\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"+/.\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a map of action counts\nfunc countChanges(changesByAction map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) map[plans.Action]int {\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, changes := range changesByAction {\n\t\tcounts[action] =     "content": "// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.\n// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchangesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\t// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\tvar output strings.Builder\n\n\t// Define the order of actions to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Process each action type in order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges, ok := changesByAction[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s resources:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceType := rc.Addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := rc.Addr.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Build the full resource address\n\t\t\tvar addr string\n\t\t\tif rc.Addr.Module.IsRoot() {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s\", resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"module.%s.%s.%s\", strings.Join(rc.Addr.Module.Module().Names(), \".\"), resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\toutput.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tcounts := countChanges(changesByAction)\n\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy\\n\",\n\t\tcounts[plans.Create]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]+counts[plans.CreateThenForget],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Update],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Delete]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete],\n\t))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete, plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// actionSymbol returns a short symbol for an action type\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"-/+\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"+/-\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"+/.\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a map of action counts\nfunc countChanges(changesByAction map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) map[plans.Action]int {\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, changes := range changesByAction {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(changes)\n\t}\n\treturn counts\n}\n",

*CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel rc.Addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := rc.Addr.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Build the full resource address\n\t\t\tvar addr string\n\t\t\tif rc.Addr.Module.IsRoot() {\n\t\t\t\taddr = output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"+/.\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a map of action counts\nfunc countChanges(changesByAction map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) map[plans.Action]int {\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, changes := range changesByAction {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(changes)\n\t}\n\treturn counts\n}\n",

1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
// attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.
// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Group changes by action type
	changesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)

	// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects
	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)
		if rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {
			continue
		}

		changesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)
	}

	var output strings.Builder

	// Define the order of actions to display
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
	}

	// Process each action type in order
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		changes, ok := changesByAction[action]
		if !ok || len(changes) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Sort resources by address for consistent output
		sort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {
			return 
... (truncated)

	"testing"
